### Overview [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/semconv/v1.32.0/k8sconv#pkg-overview "Go to Overview")

Package k8sconv provides types and functionality for OpenTelemetry semantic conventions in the "k8s" namespace.

#### type [CronJobActiveJobs](https://github.com/open-telemetry/opentelemetry-go/blob/v1.40.0/semconv/v1.32.0/k8sconv/metric.go#L55)[¶](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/semconv/v1.32.0/k8sconv#CronJobActiveJobs "Go to CronJobActiveJobs")

type CronJobActiveJobs struct {
[metric](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel/metric).[Int64UpDownCounter](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel/metric#Int64UpDownCounter)}

CronJobActiveJobs is an instrument used to record metric values conforming to the "k8s.cronjob.active_jobs" semantic conventions. It represents the number of actively running jobs for a cronjob.

#### func [NewCronJobActiveJobs](https://github.com/open-telemetry/opentelemetry-go/blob/v1.40.0/semconv/v1.32.0/k8sconv/metric.go#L60)[¶](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/semconv/v1.32.0/k8sconv#NewCronJobActiveJobs "Go to NewCronJobActiveJobs")

	m [metric](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel/metric).[Meter](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel/metric#Meter),
	opt ...[metric](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel/metric).[Int64UpDownCounterOption](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel/metric#Int64UpDownCounterOption),
) ([CronJobActiveJobs](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/semconv/v1.32.0/k8sconv#CronJobActiveJobs), [error](https://pkg.go.dev/builtin#error))

func (m [CronJobActiveJobs](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/semconv/v1.32.0/k8sconv#CronJobActiveJobs)) Add(ctx [context](https://pkg.go.dev/context).[Context](https://pkg.go.dev/context#Context), incr [int64](https://pkg.go.dev/builtin#int64), attrs ...[attribute](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/attribute).[KeyValue](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/attribute#KeyValue))

Add adds incr to the existing count.

This metric aligns with the `active` field of the [K8s CronJobStatus].

This metric SHOULD, at a minimum, be reported against a [`k8s.cronjob`] resource.

type DaemonSetCurrentScheduledNodes struct {
[metric](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel/metric).[Int64UpDownCounter](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel/metric#Int64UpDownCounter)}

DaemonSetCurrentScheduledNodes is an instrument used to record metric values conforming to the "k8s.daemonset.current_scheduled_nodes" semantic conventions. It represents the number of nodes that are running at least 1 daemon pod and are supposed to run the daemon pod.

DaemonSetDesiredScheduledNodes is an instrument used to record metric values conforming to the "k8s.daemonset.desired_scheduled_nodes" semantic conventions. It represents the number of nodes that should be running the daemon pod (including nodes currently running the daemon pod).

[metric](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel/metric).[Int64UpDownCounter](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel/metric#Int64UpDownCounter)}

DaemonSetMisscheduledNodes is an instrument used to record metric values conforming to the "k8s.daemonset.misscheduled_nodes" semantic conventions. It represents the number of nodes that are running the daemon pod, but are not supposed to run the daemon pod.

#### type [NamespacePhaseAttr](https://github.com/open-telemetry/opentelemetry-go/blob/v1.40.0/semconv/v1.32.0/k8sconv/metric.go#L26)[¶](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/semconv/v1.32.0/k8sconv#NamespacePhaseAttr "Go to NamespacePhaseAttr")

type NamespacePhaseAttr [string](https://pkg.go.dev/builtin#string)

NamespacePhaseAttr is an attribute conforming to the k8s.namespace.phase semantic conventions. It represents the phase of the K8s namespace.

var (
// NamespacePhaseActive is the active namespace phase as described by [K8s API]	// .
	//
	// [K8s API]: [https://pkg.go.dev/k8s.io/api@v0.31.3/core/v1#NamespacePhase](https://pkg.go.dev/k8s.io/api@v0.31.3/core/v1#NamespacePhase)
	NamespacePhaseActive [NamespacePhaseAttr](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/semconv/v1.32.0/k8sconv#NamespacePhaseAttr) = "active"
// NamespacePhaseTerminating is the terminating namespace phase as described by	// [K8s API].
	//
	// [K8s API]: [https://pkg.go.dev/k8s.io/api@v0.31.3/core/v1#NamespacePhase](https://pkg.go.dev/k8s.io/api@v0.31.3/core/v1#NamespacePhase)
	NamespacePhaseTerminating [NamespacePhaseAttr](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/semconv/v1.32.0/k8sconv#NamespacePhaseAttr) = "terminating"
)

func (m [NodeUptime](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/semconv/v1.32.0/k8sconv#NodeUptime)) Record(ctx [context](https://pkg.go.dev/context).[Context](https://pkg.go.dev/context#Context), val [float64](https://pkg.go.dev/builtin#float64), attrs ...[attribute](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/attribute).[KeyValue](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/attribute#KeyValue))

Record records val to the current distribution.

Instrumentations SHOULD use a gauge with type `double` and measure uptime in seconds as a floating point number with the highest precision available. The actual accuracy would depend on the instrumentation and operating system.

#### func (PodUptime) [Record](https://github.com/open-telemetry/opentelemetry-go/blob/v1.40.0/semconv/v1.32.0/k8sconv/metric.go#L2251)[¶](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/semconv/v1.32.0/k8sconv#PodUptime.Record "Go to PodUptime.Record")

func (m [PodUptime](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/semconv/v1.32.0/k8sconv#PodUptime)) Record(ctx [context](https://pkg.go.dev/context).[Context](https://pkg.go.dev/context#Context), val [float64](https://pkg.go.dev/builtin#float64), attrs ...[attribute](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/attribute).[KeyValue](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/attribute#KeyValue))

Record records val to the current distribution.

Instrumentations SHOULD use a gauge with type `double` and measure uptime in seconds as a floating point number with the highest precision available. The actual accuracy would depend on the instrumentation and operating system.

#### type [StatefulSetReadyPods](https://github.com/open-telemetry/opentelemetry-go/blob/v1.40.0/semconv/v1.32.0/k8sconv/metric.go#L2731)[¶](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/semconv/v1.32.0/k8sconv#StatefulSetReadyPods "Go to StatefulSetReadyPods")

type StatefulSetReadyPods struct {
[metric](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel/metric).[Int64UpDownCounter](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel/metric#Int64UpDownCounter)}

StatefulSetReadyPods is an instrument used to record metric values conforming to the "k8s.statefulset.ready_pods" semantic conventions. It represents the number of replica pods created for this statefulset with a Ready Condition.

#### func [NewStatefulSetReadyPods](https://github.com/open-telemetry/opentelemetry-go/blob/v1.40.0/semconv/v1.32.0/k8sconv/metric.go#L2736)[¶](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/semconv/v1.32.0/k8sconv#NewStatefulSetReadyPods "Go to NewStatefulSetReadyPods")

func NewStatefulSetReadyPods(
	m [metric](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel/metric).[Meter](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel/metric#Meter),
	opt ...[metric](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel/metric).[Int64UpDownCounterOption](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel/metric#Int64UpDownCounterOption),
) ([StatefulSetReadyPods](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/semconv/v1.32.0/k8sconv#StatefulSetReadyPods), [error](https://pkg.go.dev/builtin#error))

NewStatefulSetReadyPods returns a new StatefulSetReadyPods instrument.

#### func (StatefulSetReadyPods) [Add](https://github.com/open-telemetry/opentelemetry-go/blob/v1.40.0/semconv/v1.32.0/k8sconv/metric.go#L2788)[¶](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/semconv/v1.32.0/k8sconv#StatefulSetReadyPods.Add "Go to StatefulSetReadyPods.Add")

func (m [StatefulSetReadyPods](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/semconv/v1.32.0/k8sconv#StatefulSetReadyPods)) Add(ctx [context](https://pkg.go.dev/context).[Context](https://pkg.go.dev/context#Context), incr [int64](https://pkg.go.dev/builtin#int64), attrs ...[attribute](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/attribute).[KeyValue](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/attribute#KeyValue))

Add adds incr to the existing count.

This metric aligns with the `readyReplicas` field of the [K8s StatefulSetStatus].

This metric SHOULD, at a minimum, be reported against a [`k8s.statefulset`] resource.

[K8s StatefulSetStatus]: [https://kubernetes.io/docs/reference/generated/kubernetes-api/v1.30/#statefulsetstatus-v1-apps](https://kubernetes.io/docs/reference/generated/kubernetes-api/v1.30/#statefulsetstatus-v1-apps) [`k8s.statefulset`]: ../resource/k8s.md#statefulset

#### type [StatefulSetUpdatedPods](https://github.com/open-telemetry/opentelemetry-go/blob/v1.40.0/semconv/v1.32.0/k8sconv/metric.go#L2808)[¶](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/semconv/v1.32.0/k8sconv#StatefulSetUpdatedPods "Go to StatefulSetUpdatedPods")

type StatefulSetUpdatedPods struct {
[metric](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel/metric).[Int64UpDownCounter](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel/metric#Int64UpDownCounter)}

StatefulSetUpdatedPods is an instrument used to record metric values conforming to the "k8s.statefulset.updated_pods" semantic conventions. It represents the number of replica pods created by the statefulset controller from the statefulset version indicated by updateRevision.

#### func [NewStatefulSetUpdatedPods](https://github.com/open-telemetry/opentelemetry-go/blob/v1.40.0/semconv/v1.32.0/k8sconv/metric.go#L2813)[¶](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/semconv/v1.32.0/k8sconv#NewStatefulSetUpdatedPods "Go to NewStatefulSetUpdatedPods")

	opt ...[metric](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel/metric).[Int64UpDownCounterOption](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel/metric#Int64UpDownCounterOption),
